<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:допинг.html>до́пинг</a> (25259)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">doping</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:допинг.html>до́пинг</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">dóping</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:допинг.html>до́пинга</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:допинг.html>до́пинги</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:допинг.html>до́пингов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>stimulant, performance-enhancing drug, dope <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">any illicit drug</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:первый.html>пе́рвый</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:официальный.html>официа́льный</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:допинг.html>до́пинг</a></b>-контро́ль <a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>был</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:осуществлённый.html>осуществлён</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:во.html>во</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:время.html>вре́мя</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:олимпийский.html>олимпи́йских</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:игра.html>игр</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> грено́бле.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Pérvyj oficiálʹnyj <b>dóping</b>-kontrólʹ byl osuščestvljón vo vrémja Olimpíjskix igr v Grenóble.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">The first official <b>dope</b> control was carried out during the Olympic Games in Grenoble.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:недопить.html>до-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">do-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:писать.html>писа́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pisátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дописать.html>дописа́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">dopisátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дописывать.html>допи́сывать</a></b>)

<ol><li>to finish <i>(writing)</i></li>
<li>to write <i>(to)</i></li>
<li>to write in addition, to add</li>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:до.html>до</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:пи.html>пи</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>са́ть</b>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:дополняющий.html>дополня́ющий</a> (13784)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дополняющий.html>дополня́ющий</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">dopolnjájuščij</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">present active imperfective participle of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дополнять.html>дополня́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">dopolnjátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:допрашивать.html>допра́шивавший</a> (7191)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:допрашивать.html>допра́шивавший</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">doprášivavšij</span>)

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:допросить.html>допроси́ть</a> (11494)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:недопить.html>до-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">do-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:просить.html>проси́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">prosítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:допросить.html>допроси́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">doprosítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:допрашивать.html>допра́шивать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to interrogate
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:допросить.html>допроси́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:пристрастие.html>пристра́стием</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>doprosítʹ</b> s pristrástijem</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">dated</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> to torture; <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">jocular</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> to question in detail</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:до.html>до</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:про.html>про</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>си́ть</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:переходный.html>перехо́дный</a>,    <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. <p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:недопить.html>до-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">do-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пускать.html>пуска́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">puskátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<ol><li>to admit</li>
<li>to accept, to permit, to allow, to tolerate</li>
<li>to assume

<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́того</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:нельзя.html>нельзя́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:допускать.html>допуска́ть</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">étovo nelʹzjá <b>dopuskátʹ</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">this cannot be tolerated</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>его́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:допустить.html>допусти́ли</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>к</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:экзамен.html>экза́менам</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">jevó ne dopustíli k ekzámenam</i> ― <span class="e-translation">he was not admitted to the test</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:допустить.html>допусти́ть</a> (2617)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:недопить.html>до-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">do-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пустить.html>пусти́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pustítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:допустить.html>допусти́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">dopustítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:допускать.html>допуска́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to admit</li>
<li>to permit, to allow, to tolerate</li>
<li>to assume
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>он</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:допускать.html>допуска́ет</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:этот.html>э́той</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мысль.html>мы́сли</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">on ne <b>dopuskájet</b> étoj mýsli</i> ― <span class="e-translation">he thinks it’s impossible</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́того</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:нельзя.html>нельзя́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:допускать.html>допуска́ть</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">étovo nelʹzjá <b>dopuskátʹ</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">it cannot be tolerated</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>его́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:допустить.html>допусти́ли</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>к</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:экзамен.html>экза́менам</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">jevó ne <b>dopustíli</b> k ekzámenam</i> ― <span class="e-translation">he was not allowed to take the examinations</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:допустимый.html>допу́стим</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>dopústim</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">let's assume; (let's) say; for example</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
